foſters verders geſt taker none dyſtres thyrd ſwanymote ſhalbe kept begynnyng xv dayes feaſte ſaynct iohan baptyſte geſt taker walker mete hunte deere ſwanymote ſhall mete foſters verders none dyſtres great men engelande whiche haue infeffed knyghtes theyr freholders ſmall tenementes theyr great maners haue complayned haue profyte ye reſydue theyr maners waſte woodes paſtures becauſe ſame feffees ought haue ſufficient paſture accordyng theyr holde thus prouyded graū • ed whan ſo euer ſuche feffees • brynge aſſyſe nouell dyſſeſon theyr comē paſture knowleged iuſtyces haue almoch paſture countre clauſe muſte added et diligenter inquiras vbi ille here ſit balliua tua et ipſum vbicunque inuenius fuerit capias et ſaluo et ſecure cuſtodias ita quod cum habeas corā pre • atis iuſticiatus noſtris ad prefa • um terminum ad reddendum cui predictorum et b reddi debeat ſute ſhalbe made agaynſte partye defendant vntyll come dyſ treſſe haue wherof may dyſtrayned wyll iuſtefyed ſhalbe talus loco comitatu talus rapuit et de comitatu illo ad talem locum comitatu tuo abduxit contra voluntatem ipſius et contra pacem c et ideo tibi precipimus quod predictum heredem vbicunque cum balliua tua inuenire poteris capias et ſaluo et ſecure eum cuſtodias ita quod cum habeas corā iuſticiarus noſtris c talus die qu • idem habet verſus predictum b ad reddendum cui de iure reddi debeat heyre kynges prohybicyon ſhal holde place moreouer lay vyolent handes clerke amendes vyolence done ſhall made kynges cour • e excommunicacyon prelate penaunce corporall enioyned defendour wyll redeme penaunce gyuynge money prelate partye greued ſhalbe requyred prelate kynges prohybicyon ſhall lye dyffamacyons alſo prelate ſhall correcte maner aboue ſayd kynges prohybicyon notwithſtandynge fyrſte enioynynge penaunce corporal offendour wyll redeme prelate maye frely receyue money though kynges prohybicyon ſhewed alſo arere grounde mylle newe perſone ſame prelate demaundyth tythe ſame kynges prohybicyon doth iſſue fourme aunſwere quia de talus molendino hactenus decime non fuerunt ſolute prohibemus c et ſententiam excommunicationis ſi quam hac occaſione promulgaueritis ••• e • omnino ſuche caſe kynges wrytte prohybicyon neuer yet graunted kynges aſſente neuer ſhall whiche hath decreyd ſhall hereafter ſuche caſes alſo cauſe mattyer knowledge wherof belongyth courte ſpirituall dyffynytyfly determyned ſpyrytuall iudge ſo paſſe iudgement ſuſpens reaſon appeall afterwarde vpon ſame thynge caſe moued • temporal iudge betwene ſame partyes prouyd wytnes inſtrumentes excepcyon ſhall admytted temporall court aunſwere one caſe debated iudges ſpirituall temporall aboue aperyth vpon caſe layenge violent h • de clerke thought notwithſtandyng ſpirituall iudgement kynges court ſhall dyſcuſſe • ſame matter party ſhall thynk moſt expedyē • hymſelfe alſo kynges lettre dyrected vnto ordinaryes haue wrapped theyr clyentes ſentence • xcommunicacyon ſhulde aſſeyle certayne daye church put newe kynges counſell kyng auncetours ſyns tyme mynde haue vſed clerkes duryng ſuch tyme ſeruyce ſhal compelled vnto kepe reſydence theyr benefyces ſuch thynges thought neceſſary kynge comon welth ought called preiudicyall lyberte churche alſo kinges offycers ſheryfes entre ſpirituall fee take diſtreſſes ſometyme take perſones beſtes kynges hyghe way haue nothynge theyr glebe lande aunſwere kynges pleaſure hensforth ſuch dyſtreſſes ſhall neyther taken kynges hygh way fee wherwith church haue ben indowed neuer theleſſe wylleth dyſtreſſes taken poſſeſſions church newly purchaſed perſone alſo flye vnto churche abiure realme accordynge cuſtome lande laye men theyr ennemyes purſue plucke kynges hygh waye hanged heded whylſt churche kepte churchyard armed men ſometyme churche ſo ſtraytly departe halowed grounde emptye theyr belye ſuffred haue neceſſaryes theyr lyuyng thaunſwer abiure realme ſo long comen waye ſhalbe kynges peace ſhalbe dyſtourbed man churche theyr kepars ought abyde churchyarde excepte neceſſyte peryll eſcape requyre ſo ſo longe churche ſhall compelled auoyde ſhall haue neceſſaryes theyr lyuynge may go forth emptye theyr belye alſo kynges pleaſure theues appellours ſo euer wyl may confeſſe theyr offenſes vnto preſtes let confeſſours beware infourme ſuch appeallours vnwarely alſo deſyred ſoueraygne lorde kynge great men realme charge relygyous
